#Civil Defence - Nuke Protection - Start
country_event = {
	id = 1412169
	title = "Nuclear Shelters Activated"
	desc = EVTDESC1412169
	picture = "nuclear_shelter"

	trigger = { 
	
		#Country has been hit by nuclear weapons
		any_owned_province = { 
			OR = { 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_high 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_medium 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_low 
			} 
		}
		
		#Has some proper Civil Defence
		OR = { 
			has_country_modifier = cdhigh 
			has_country_modifier = cdmedium 
		}
		
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nuke_protection }
	}

	option = {
		name = "A moment of silence for those who didn't make it"
		
		set_country_flag = nuke_protection

		#High Civil Defence
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = cdhigh } } 
			owner = { 
				any_owned = { 
					limit = { has_province_modifier = nuke_low } 
					remove_province_modifier = nuke_low
					add_province_modifier = { name = nuke_low duration = 9125 } 
				} 
				any_owned = { 
					limit = { has_province_modifier = nuke_medium } 
					remove_province_modifier = nuke_medium
					add_province_modifier = { name = nuke_low duration = 18250 } 
				} 
				any_owned = { 
					limit = { has_province_modifier = nuke_high } 
					remove_province_modifier = nuke_high
					add_province_modifier = { name = nuke_medium duration = 18250 } 
				} 
			} 
		}
		
		#Medium Civil Defence - Only protects against medium nuke damage at best
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = cdhigh } } 
			owner = { 
				any_owned = { 
					limit = { has_province_modifier = nuke_low } 
					remove_province_modifier = nuke_low
					add_province_modifier = { name = nuke_low duration = 9125 } 
				} 
				any_owned = { 
					limit = { has_province_modifier = nuke_medium } 
					remove_province_modifier = nuke_medium
					add_province_modifier = { name = nuke_low duration = 18250 } 
				} 
			} 
		}

	}

}

#Civil Defence - No Nuke Protection - Total Anarchy!
country_event = {
	id = 14121691
	title = "Anarchy in $COUNTRY$"
	desc = EVTDESC14121691
	picture = "nuclear_fallout_anarchy"

	trigger = { 
	
		#Country has been hit by nuclear weapons
		any_owned_province = { 
			OR = { 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_high 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_medium 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_low 
			} 
		}
		
		#Has no Civil Defence
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				has_country_modifier = cdhigh 
				has_country_modifier = cdmedium 
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nuke_protection }
	}

	option = {
		name = "A moment of silence for those who didn't make it"
		
		set_country_flag = nuke_protection

		#All provinces get transferred to rebels
		any_owned = {
			limit = { controlled_by = THIS }
			change_controller = REB
		}

	}

}

#Civil Defence - states occassionally fall to rebels
country_event = {
	id = 14121692
	title = "Government Control Weakens"
	desc = EVTDESC14121692
	picture = "nuclear_fallout_anarchy_2"

	trigger = { 
	
		#Country has been hit by nuclear weapons
		any_owned_province = { 
			OR = { 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_high 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_medium 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_low 
			} 
			controlled_by = THIS
			average_militancy = 9
		}
		
		#Has weak civil defence
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = cdhigh }
		
		#Post nuclear government
		has_country_flag = nuke_protection
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6
	}

	option = {
		name = "At this rate we might lose the whole country!"
		prestige_factor = -0.01
		
		#Transfer states to rebels
		any_owned = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					has_province_modifier = nuke_high 
					has_province_modifier = nuke_medium 
					has_province_modifier = nuke_low 
				} 
				controlled_by = THIS
				average_militancy = 9
			}
			state_scope = {
				any_owned = {
					limit = { 
						is_state_capital = no 
						controlled_by = THIS 
					}
					change_controller = REB
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

#Zimbabwe Name
country_event = {
	id = 1412207
	title = "Transition to Zimbabwe"
	desc = EVTDESC1412207	
	picture = "zimbabwe_name"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = { 
		tag = ZIM
		OR = { government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 }
		war = no
		election = no
		OR = { 
			is_vassal = no
			
			#Landcaster House Agreement
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = RHO_ENG_revert_flag
				vassal_of = ENG
			} 
		}
		
		OR = { 
			AND = { year = 1980 has_country_flag = RHO_ENG_revert_flag }
			
			#5 years slower if no British help
			AND = { year = 1985 NOT = { has_country_flag = RHO_ENG_revert_flag } }
		}
		
		NOT = { primary_culture = shona }
		
		NOT = { minorities_reform = minorities_oppression }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4
	}

	option = {
		name = "End white rule once and for all!"
		
		#If Landcaster House Agreement was accepted, option for ENG to grant independence
		overlord = { country_event = 8012217 }
		
		government = democracy
		prestige = 50
		primary_culture = shona
		add_accepted_culture = british
		ruling_party_ideology = socialist
		
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_primary_culture = shona }
			militancy = -10
			ideology = { factor = 0.30 value = socialist }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = { OR = { primary_culture = british accepted_culture = british } } 
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -50 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.8 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Stay as Zimbabwe-Rhodesia"
		any_pop = { limit = { is_primary_culture = no } militancy = 5 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = revolution_chaos duration = 3650 }

		random_country = { 
			limit = { OR = { primary_culture = british accepted_culture = british } } 
			relation = { who = THIS value = 50 }
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = 25 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.2 }
	}

}

#Keep the Empire - All Colonial Provinces add modifier
country_event = {
	id = 1412217
	title = "Dissent in the $COUNTRY_ADJ$ Colonies"
	desc = EVTDESC1412217
	picture = "colonial_dissent"

	trigger = {
	
		#Blocking decolonisation events
		has_country_flag = decolonise_yes

		#Oppressing minorities
		minorities_reform = minorities_oppression

		#Has colonial provinces without the dissent province modifier
		any_owned_province = { 
			NOT = { is_core = THIS } 
			is_colonial = yes 
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = decolonise_yes } 
		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6
	}

	option = {
		name = "A necessary evil to preserve the empire"
		badboy = 1
		prestige = -10
		any_owned = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_core = THIS } 
				
				#Colonial provinces only
				is_colonial = yes 
				
				#Province must not be majority accepted culture
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
				
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = decolonise_yes } 
			} 
			add_province_modifier = { name = decolonise_yes duration = -1 } 
		}
	}

}

#Keep the Empire - Remove Province Modifier (province event)
province_event = {
	id = 1412218
	title = "Anti-Colonial Dissent Eases in $STATENAME$"
	desc = EVTDESC1412218
	picture = "dissant_reduce"

	trigger = {
	
		#Has colonial dissent modifier
		has_province_modifier = decolonise_yes

		#Owner blocking decolonisation events
		owner = { has_country_flag = decolonise_yes }
		
		#Only fires in the state capital
		is_state_capital = yes
		
		OR = {
			#Owner is not oppressing minorities
			owner = { NOT = { minorities_reform = minorities_oppression } }
		
			#Don't have a lot of radical natives sitting around
			AND = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
				NOT = { populist = 0.10 }
				NOT = { nationalist = 0.10 }
				NOT = { traditionalist = 0.10 }
				NOT = { socialist = 0.15 }
				NOT = { communist = 0.10 }
				NOT = { communist_social = 0.10 }
			}
			
			#This province is no longer colonial
			is_colonial = no
			
			#Natives have been diluted off from province
			is_primary_culture = yes
			is_accepted_culture = yes
		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 400
	}

	option = {
		name = "Excellent news!"
		state_scope = { 
			any_owned = { 
				remove_province_modifier = decolonise_yes 
				any_pop = { militancy = -5 consciousness = -5 }
			} 
		}
	}

}

#Keep the Empire - Gain Legitimacy in province with primary or accepted pop as majority ideology
country_event = {
	id = 1412219
	title = "Legitimacy Gained Over Certain Provinces"
	desc = EVTDESC1412219
	picture = "gain_colony_core"

	trigger = {
	
		#Active attempt to artificially core provinces
		OR = { 
			has_country_flag = pop_displacement_system_active 
			has_country_flag = promote_colonial_migration_active
			has_country_flag = population_replacement_underway
		}
	
		is_vassal = no
		war = no
		
		#THIS is not an international pariah
		NOT = { badboy = 1 }
		
		#Has eligible provinces
		any_owned_province = {
		
			#Not already a core of THIS
			NOT = { is_core = THIS }
		
			#THIS controls the province
			controlled_by = THIS
			
			#Province has either majority primary or accepted culture
			OR = {
				is_primary_culture = yes
				is_accepted_culture = yes
			}
			
		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 12
	}

	option = {
		name = "It's about time!"
		prestige = 10
		
		#Add cores to uncored provinces
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				#Not already a core of THIS
				NOT = { is_core = THIS }
		
				#THIS controls the province
				controlled_by = THIS
			
				#Province has either majority primary or accepted culture
				OR = {
					is_primary_culture = yes
					is_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			state_scope = { 
				any_owned = { add_core = THIS }
			}
		}
		
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = 1413225

war = no

election = no 

OR = { election = yes NOT = { average_militancy = 3 } }

has_country_modifier = martial_law

}

months = 3
modifier = { factor = 0 election = yes }

	}

name = "Return to normality"

#Call to join superstate
country_event = {
	id = 1610001
	title = "Foundation of $COUNTRY$"
	desc = EVTDESC1610001
	picture = "superstate_formation_event"

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = XGC
			tag = XEF
			tag = XEU
			tag = XCC
			tag = XAU
			tag = XEW
			tag = XEC
			tag = XSA
			tag = XSU
			tag = XMS
			tag = XAC
			tag = XAL
			tag = XMU
			tag = XAN
			tag = XCI
			tag = XNA
			tag = XPI
			tag = XEA
			tag = XTC
			tag = XUM
			tag = XIO
		}
		war = no
		is_vassal = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = superstate_formation_event }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Congratulations to ourselves!"
		prestige = 500

		#Invitations are continent bound
		#Rules for annexation: Spheres only get annexed if they are in the same continent, not a mandate and did not lose a war recently
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
				continent = europe
			} 
			owner = { 
				any_country = { 
					limit = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								government = mandate_government
								has_recently_lost_war = yes
							}
						}
						capital_scope = { continent = europe }
					}
					country_event = 1610002
				}
			}
		}

		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
				continent = asia
			} 
			owner = { 
				any_country = { 
					limit = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								government = mandate_government
								has_recently_lost_war = yes
							}
						}
						capital_scope = { continent = asia }
					}
					country_event = 1610002
				}
			}
		}

		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
				continent = africa
			} 
			owner = { 
				any_country = { 
					limit = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								government = mandate_government
								has_recently_lost_war = yes
							}
						}
						capital_scope = { continent = africa }
					}
					country_event = 1610002
				}
			}
		}

		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
				continent = mena
			} 
			owner = { 
				any_country = { 
					limit = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								government = mandate_government
								has_recently_lost_war = yes
							}
						}
						capital_scope = { continent = mena }
					}
					country_event = 1610002
				}
			}
		}

		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
				continent = north_america
			} 
			owner = { 
				any_country = { 
					limit = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								government = mandate_government
								has_recently_lost_war = yes
							}
						}
						capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
					}
					country_event = 1610002
				}
			}
		}

		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
				continent = south_america
			} 
			owner = { 
				any_country = { 
					limit = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								government = mandate_government
								has_recently_lost_war = yes
							}
						}
						capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
					}
					country_event = 1610002
				}
			}
		}

		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
				continent = oceania
			} 
			owner = { 
				any_country = { 
					limit = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								government = mandate_government
								has_recently_lost_war = yes
							}
						}
						capital_scope = { continent = oceania }
					}
					country_event = 1610002
				}
			}
		}

		#Vassals get fully incorporated into the superstate but only if the vassal is not a mandate, did not lose a war and has the superstate's (THIS) cores in their capital
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				vassal_of = THIS
				capital_scope = { is_core = THIS }
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						government = mandate_government
						has_recently_lost_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = 11101
		}
		set_country_flag = superstate_formation_event
	}

}

#Call to join superstate
country_event = {
	id = 1610002
	title = "Union with $FROMCOUNTRY$?"
	desc = EVTDESC1610002
	picture = "superstate_formation_event"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "We shall unite!"
		all_core = { add_core = FROM }
		any_owned = {
                secede_province = FROM
        }
        FROM = { inherit = THIS }
		FROM = { prestige = 50 country_event = 11107 }
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } }

				NOT = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Stay out of the union!"
		relation = { who = FROM value = -50 }
		FROM = { diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}

}

#Supreme Court pick
country_event = {
	id = 1610012
	title = "New Supreme Court Judge"
	desc = EVTDESC1610012
	picture = "supreme_court_pick"

	trigger = {
		war = no
		OR = { 
			government = democracy 
			government = democracy1 
			government = hms_government 
			government = hms_government1 
			government = socialist_democracy 
		}
		is_vassal = no
		NOT = { civil_service = independent_service }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 120
	}

	option = {
		name = "Let an independent select committee decide"
		any_pop = { consciousness = 1 }
		
		#Affect the judiciary according to the pop majority ideology
		clr_country_flag = activist_judiciary_flag
		clr_country_flag = textualist_judiciary_flag
		remove_country_modifier = activist_judiciary
		remove_country_modifier = textualist_judiciary
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal pop_majority_ideology = progressive pop_majority_ideology = big_tent } }
			}
			owner = { 
				set_country_flag = activist_judiciary_flag 
				add_country_modifier = { name = activist_judiciary duration = 730 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = conservative pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = populist } }
			}
			owner = { 
				set_country_flag = textualist_judiciary_flag 
				add_country_modifier = { name = textualist_judiciary duration = 730 }
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Select a pro-government judge"
		
		#Affect the judiciary according to the ideology of the court
		clr_country_flag = activist_judiciary_flag
		clr_country_flag = textualist_judiciary_flag
		remove_country_modifier = activist_judiciary
		remove_country_modifier = textualist_judiciary
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = progressive ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			}
			owner = { 
				set_country_flag = activist_judiciary_flag 
				add_country_modifier = { name = activist_judiciary duration = 730 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
			}
			owner = { 
				set_country_flag = textualist_judiciary_flag 
				add_country_modifier = { name = textualist_judiciary duration = 730 }
			}
		}
		
		#Politicise Civil Service
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { civil_service = elitist_service } }
			owner = { political_reform = politicised_service }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { civil_service = professional_service } }
			owner = { political_reform = elitist_service }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { civil_service = independent_service } }
			owner = { political_reform = professional_service }
		}

		#Increase the ideology lean of bureaucrats
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = traditionalist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = conservative } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = liberal } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = big_tent } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = progressive } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = socialist } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist_social } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = nationalist } } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = populist } } }
		}
 	
		#Increase upper house support
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = traditionalist value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = conservative value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = liberal value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = big_tent value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = progressive value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = socialist value = 0.25 } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = communist value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = communist_social value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = nationalist value = 0.25 } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
			owner = { upper_house = { ideology = populist value = 0.25 } }
		}
		
		#Increase militancy and consciousness
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = traditionalist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = traditionalist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = conservative } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = conservative } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = liberal } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = liberal } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = big_tent } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = big_tent } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = progressive } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = progressive } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = socialist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = socialist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = communist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = communist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = communist_social } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = communist_social } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = nationalist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = nationalist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = populist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = populist } } } }

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }

	}

NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak } }
NOT = { has_country_modifier = local_epidemic }
NOT = { has_country_flag = ebola_outbreak_2013 }
}

}

		}

#Install friendly Absolute Monarchy
country_event = {
	id = 1610020
title = "The New Monarchist Regime"
	desc = EVT_96088_DESC
	picture = "monarchy_cleanup"

is_triggered_only = yes

option = {
name = "We have no choice but to welcome our new King"

government = absolute_monarchy 
country_event = 800050

random_country = { 
limit = { is_sphere_leader_of = THIS NOT = { has_country_flag = friendly_authoritarian_regime } }
diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -200 }
}

random_country = {

country_event = {
	id = 1610026
	title = "SARS Virus Epidemic"
	desc = EVTDESC1610026
	picture = "sars_outbreak_2003"

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		year = 2002
		NOT = { year = 2020 }
		any_owned_province = { OR = { is_core = CAN is_core = CHI is_core = HKG is_core = MCA is_core = KMT is_core = SNG is_core = DAI is_core = USA is_core = PHI is_core = MGL is_core = KUW is_core = IRE is_core = ROM is_core = RUS is_core = SPA is_core = SWI is_core = SKO } }
		NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak } }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = local_epidemic }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = sars_outbreak_2003 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 11
	}

	option = {
		name = "Try to cover it up!"
		set_country_flag = sars_outbreak_2003
		
		set_global_flag = epidemic_start
		
		CHI = { set_country_flag = virus_originator_country }
		
		set_country_flag = enable_virus_controls
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		
		any_country = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.8 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Do everything we can to stop the outbreak!"
		set_country_flag = sars_outbreak_2003

		money = -300000

		set_global_flag = epidemic_start
		
		CHI = { set_country_flag = virus_originator_country }
		
		set_country_flag = enable_virus_controls
		
		set_country_flag = who_alerted_to_new_virus
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		
		any_country = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.2 }
	}

}

			}
			
		}

			AND = {

limit = { owner = { OR = { has_country_modifier = hydrogen_nation has_country_modifier = atomic_nation } } }
owner = { set_country_flag = can_take_nukes } 
}

limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = chemical_nation } }
owner = { set_country_flag = can_take_chemical } 
}

owner = { set_country_flag = can_take_biological } 
}

clr_country_flag = hydrogen_bomb_developed
clr_country_flag = icbm_bomb
clr_country_flag = sub_bomb
clr_country_flag = air_bomb

clr_country_flag = choking_bomb
clr_country_flag = blister_bomb
remove_country_modifier = chemical_sanctions
remove_country_modifier = chemical_nation
remove_country_modifier = develop_chemical_bomb 
clr_country_flag = chemical_bomb_developed

#Remove Biological modifiers

		}

}

#Interfere with sphere politics - independent
country_event = {
	id = 1610042
	title = "Foreign Interference in $COUNTRY_ADJ$ Politics"
	desc = EVTDESC1610042
	picture = "interfering_with_sphere"

	trigger = {
		part_of_sphere = yes
		sphere_owner = { has_country_modifier = sphere_interference }
		is_vassal = no

		OR = { 

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_traditionalist } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_conservative } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_big_tent } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_socialist } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_communist } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_communist_social } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_populist } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_nationalist } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_liberal } }

			AND = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } NOT = { has_country_flag = sphere_progressive } }

		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6
	}

	option = {
		name = "We can't do anything"
		prestige_factor = -0.01
		sphere_owner = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } }

		clr_country_flag = sphere_traditionalist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_conservative
		clr_country_flag = sphere_big_tent
		clr_country_flag = sphere_socialist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_communist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_communist_social
		clr_country_flag = sphere_populist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_nationalist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_liberal
		clr_country_flag = sphere_progressive

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_traditionalist } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_conservative } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_big_tent } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_socialist } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_communist } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_communist_social } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_populist } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_nationalist } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_liberal } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { sphere_owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } } owner = { set_country_flag = sphere_progressive } }

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					sphere_owner = { 
						OR = { 
							ruling_party_ideology = nationalist 
							ruling_party_ideology = populist 
							alliance_with = THIS 
							relation = { who = THIS value = 50 } 
						} 
					}
					OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist } 
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Sever ties with our sphere master!"
		sphere_owner = { relation = { who = THIS value = -200 } diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -200 } }

		clr_country_flag = sphere_traditionalist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_conservative
		clr_country_flag = sphere_big_tent
		clr_country_flag = sphere_socialist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_communist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_communist_social
		clr_country_flag = sphere_populist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_nationalist
		clr_country_flag = sphere_liberal
		clr_country_flag = sphere_progressive

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				AND = {
					sphere_owner = { 
						NOT = { 
							OR = { 
								ruling_party_ideology = nationalist 
								ruling_party_ideology = populist 
								alliance_with = THIS 
								relation = { who = THIS value = 50 } 
							} 
						}
					}
					NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist } } 
				}
			} 
		}
	}

}

#Backbencher's plot - constitutional monarchies or parliamentary republics
country_event = {
	id = 1610048
	title = "Backbencher's Plot"
	desc = EVTDESC1610048
	picture = "backbenchers_plot"

	trigger = {

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = leader_cooldown }

		NOT = { has_country_flag = leader_refuses_to_leave }

		election = no

		average_militancy = 4

		OR = { 

			has_country_modifier = ruling_party_scandal 
			average_militancy = 5

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = conservative } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = big_tent } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = socialist } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = communist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = communist } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = communist_social } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = populist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = populist } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = progressive } }

			AND = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal } }

		}

		OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 has_country_flag = parliamentary_system_republic }

		war = no

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = nepohigh }

		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = expert_diplomat
			has_country_modifier = successful_industrialist
			has_country_modifier = ivory_tower_intellectual
			has_country_modifier = man_of_the_people
			has_country_modifier = landed_gentleman
			has_country_modifier = military_man
			has_country_modifier = lord_admiral
			has_country_modifier = raving_loon
			has_country_modifier = luddite
			has_country_modifier = great_statesman
			has_country_modifier = backroom_boy
			has_country_modifier = great_reformer
			has_country_modifier = gauche_buffoon
			has_country_modifier = administrative_genius
			has_country_modifier = visionary_thinker
			has_country_modifier = competent_placeholder
			has_country_modifier = imperious_autocrat
			has_country_modifier = prince_of_terror
			has_country_modifier = efficient_sociopath
			has_country_modifier = pig_headed_isolationist
			has_country_modifier = ambitious_union_boss
			has_country_modifier = dour_economist
			has_country_modifier = power_vacuum
		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6

		modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_modifier = nepomedium }
		modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { average_militancy = 3 } }
		modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { average_militancy = 2 } }
		modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { average_militancy = 1 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Accept their demands"

		country_event = 111222

		any_pop = { militancy = -2 consciousness = -2 }

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.75 }
	}

option = {
name = "Refuse to leave!"

prestige_factor = -0.01

any_pop = { militancy = 2 consciousness = 2 }

add_country_modifier = { name = leadership_chaos duration = 100 }

set_country_flag = leader_refuses_to_leave

#Chance of starting military unrest
random_owned = {
limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = military_loyalty_low } }
owner = {
random = {
	chance = 35
	country_event = 100100
}
	}
}

#Backbencher's plot - dictatorship
country_event = {
	id = 1610049
title = "Conspiracy to oust the $MONARCHTITLE$"
	desc = EVTDESC1610049
	picture = "politburo_plot"

trigger = {

NOT = { has_country_modifier = leader_cooldown }

NOT = { has_country_flag = leader_refuses_to_leave }

NOT = { AND = { has_global_flag = blocsenabled ai = yes OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } } }

average_militancy = 5

OR = { 

any_pop = { type = bureaucrats average_militancy = 8 }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = conservative } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = big_tent } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = socialist } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = communist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = communist } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = communist_social } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = populist NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = populist } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = progressive } }

AND = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal } }

}

OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = nationalist_dictatorship government = sectarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 government = theocracy }

war = no

NOT = { has_country_modifier = nepohigh }

OR = {
has_country_modifier = expert_diplomat
has_country_modifier = successful_industrialist
has_country_modifier = ivory_tower_intellectual
has_country_modifier = man_of_the_people
has_country_modifier = landed_gentleman
has_country_modifier = military_man
has_country_modifier = lord_admiral
has_country_modifier = raving_loon
has_country_modifier = luddite
has_country_modifier = great_statesman
has_country_modifier = backroom_boy
has_country_modifier = great_reformer
has_country_modifier = gauche_buffoon
has_country_modifier = administrative_genius
has_country_modifier = visionary_thinker
has_country_modifier = competent_placeholder
has_country_modifier = imperious_autocrat
has_country_modifier = prince_of_terror
has_country_modifier = efficient_sociopath
has_country_modifier = pig_headed_isolationist
has_country_modifier = ambitious_union_boss
has_country_modifier = dour_economist
has_country_modifier = power_vacuum
	}

}

mean_time_to_happen = { 
months = 3

modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_modifier = nepomedium }

modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { average_militancy = 3 } }

}

option = {
name = "Accept their demands"

#Congress to select new dictator
country_event = 1412075

#If leader refused to leave via 'backbencher's plot' event
clr_country_flag = leader_refuses_to_leave

#Remove existing leaders modifiers

		remove_country_modifier = expert_diplomat
		remove_country_modifier = successful_industrialist
		remove_country_modifier = ivory_tower_intellectual
		remove_country_modifier = man_of_the_people
		remove_country_modifier = landed_gentleman
		remove_country_modifier = military_man
		remove_country_modifier = lord_admiral
		remove_country_modifier = raving_loon
		remove_country_modifier = luddite
		remove_country_modifier = great_statesman
		remove_country_modifier = backroom_boy
		remove_country_modifier = great_reformer
		remove_country_modifier = gauche_buffoon
		remove_country_modifier = administrative_genius
		remove_country_modifier = visionary_thinker
		remove_country_modifier = competent_placeholder
		remove_country_modifier = imperious_autocrat
		remove_country_modifier = prince_of_terror
		remove_country_modifier = efficient_sociopath
		remove_country_modifier = pig_headed_isolationist
		remove_country_modifier = ambitious_union_boss
		remove_country_modifier = dour_economist

clr_country_flag = right_set_up
clr_country_flag = far_right_set_up
clr_country_flag = centre_set_up
clr_country_flag = left_set_up
clr_country_flag = far_left_set_up

#Pop militancy effects

any_pop = { militancy = -2 }

any_pop = { limit = { type = bureaucrats } militancy = -5 }

ai_chance = { factor = 0.75 }
		}

option = {
name = "Refuse to leave!"

prestige_factor = -0.01

	country_event = 100100

any_owned_province = { continent = africa }

#Straits of Malacca
any_owned_province = { 
OR = { is_core = MSY is_core = IDO is_core = SNG }
	} 

}

	}

months = 60
	}

	}

}

#Import Substitution Economy in South America
country_event = {
	id = 1610061
title = "Import Substitution Economy in $COUNTRY$?"
	desc = EVTDESC1610061
	picture = "south_america_isi"

trigger = {
OR = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } tag = MEX }
year = 1946
NOT = { year = 1990 }
is_vassal = no
election = no
war = no

NOT = { has_country_flag = south_american_isi }
NOT = { has_country_flag = south_american_isi_event_fired }
	}

mean_time_to_happen = { 
months = 1
	}

option = {
name = "Embrace this magical way"

set_country_flag = south_american_isi_event_fired

add_country_modifier = { name = economic_boom duration = 5840 }

set_country_flag = south_american_isi

set_country_flag = importfocus
any_owned = { limit = { is_colonial = no } add_province_modifier = { name = importsubstitutionfocus duration = -1 } }

clr_country_flag = exportfocus
any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = exportfocus }

ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}

option = {
name = "Focus on exports instead"

set_country_flag = south_american_isi_event_fired

set_country_flag = exportfocus
any_owned = { limit = { is_colonial = no } add_province_modifier = { name = exportfocus duration = -1 } }

clr_country_flag = importfocus
any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = importsubstitutionfocus }

ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}

#Hardliners demand reform rollback
country_event = {
	id = 1610091
	title = "Party Hardliners Condemn the $MONARCHTITLE$"
	desc = EVTDESC1610091
	picture = "angry_hardliners"

	trigger = {
		ai = no
		war = no

		NOT = { num_of_revolts = 1 }

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = political_strife }

		OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 government = presidential_dictatorship government = nationalist_dictatorship government = sectarian_dictatorship }

		OR = { 
			NOT = { vote_franschise = none_voting } 
			NOT = { political_opinions = ruling_party_opinion } 
			NOT = { public_meetings = no_meetings } 
			NOT = { publishing_rights = state_publishing }
			NOT = { political_parties = parties_not_allowed }
		}

		#Angry officers or bureaucrats
		any_owned_province = {
			is_core = THIS
			any_pop = { OR = { type = officers type = bureaucrats } militancy = 8 }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 12
		modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_modifier = nepohigh }
		modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_modifier = nepolow }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Give in to their demands"
		political_reform = none_voting
		political_reform = ruling_party_opinion
		political_reform = no_meetings
		political_reform = state_publishing
		political_reform = parties_not_allowed
		any_pop = { consciousness = -2 militancy = -1 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.3
			modifier = { factor = 1 militancy = 7 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Tolerate their insolence"
		add_country_modifier = { name = political_strife duration = 730 }
		any_pop = { consciousness = 2 militancy = 1 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Purge them"
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { OR = { type = officers type = bureaucrats } militancy = 8 }
			pop_type = clerks
		}
		any_pop = { militancy = -3 consciousness = -5 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.2 }
	}

}

#Ensure UH majority during state of emergency
country_event = {
	id = 1610099
	title = "Attempt to Curtail Emergency Powers"
	desc = EVTDESC1610099
	picture = "i_am_the_senate"

	trigger = {
		has_country_modifier = martial_law
		
		election = no
		
		OR = { 
			government = democracy

			government = hms_government 
			government = hms_government1 
			government = socialist_democracy 
			government = colonial_government 
			government = mandate_government 
			government = sar_government 
		}
		
		OR = { 
		
			AND = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist
				NOT = { upper_house = { ideology = traditionalist value = 0.50 } }
			}
			
			AND = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = conservative
				NOT = { upper_house = { ideology = conservative value = 0.50 } }
			}
			
			AND = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = big_tent
				NOT = { upper_house = { ideology = big_tent value = 0.50 } }
			}
			
			AND = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = populist
				NOT = { upper_house = { ideology = populist value = 0.50 } }
			}
			
			AND = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = nationalist
				NOT = { upper_house = { ideology = nationalist value = 0.50 } }
			}
			
			AND = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = socialist
				NOT = { upper_house = { ideology = socialist value = 0.50 } }
			}

#Constitutional Conference
country_event = {
	id = 1610102
	title = "New Republican Constitution of $YEAR$"
	desc = "EVTDESC1610102"
	picture = "constitutional_conference_republic"

	trigger = {
		OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = presidential_system_republic
				has_country_flag = semi_presidential_system_republic
				has_country_flag = parliamentary_system_republic
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Use a presidential system"
		set_country_flag = presidential_system_republic
		add_country_modifier = { name = changecentral duration = 1825 }
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0.4 
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = { 
						part_of_sphere = yes 
						sphere_owner = { 
							OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = presidential_system_republic }
						}
					}
					
					AND = { 
						is_vassal = yes 
						overlord = { 
							OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = presidential_system_republic }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Use a semi-presidential system"
		set_country_flag = semi_presidential_system_republic
		add_country_modifier = { name = changecentral duration = 1825 }
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0.3
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = { 
						part_of_sphere = yes 
						sphere_owner = { 
							OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = semi_presidential_system_republic }
						}
					}
					
					AND = { 
						is_vassal = yes 
						overlord = { 
							OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = semi_presidential_system_republic }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Use a parliamentary system"
		set_country_flag = parliamentary_system_republic
		add_country_modifier = { name = changecentral duration = 1825 }
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0.3
			
			#ex Westminister colony
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				part_of_sphere = yes
				sphere_owner = {
					OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { 
					OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 }
				}
			}
			
			#Others
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = { 
						part_of_sphere = yes 
						sphere_owner = { 
							OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = parliamentary_system_republic }
						}
					}
					
					AND = { 
						is_vassal = yes 
						overlord = { 
							OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = parliamentary_system_republic }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

#FROM requests volunteer
country_event = {
	id = 1610103
	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ Requests Volunteers"
	desc = "EVTDESC1610103"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "Send a military force to aid the $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ war effort!"
		war_exhaustion = 5
		#Subtract soldiers
		any_pop = {
			limit = { type = soldiers }
			reduce_pop = 0.95
		}
		#Subtract officers
		any_pop = {
			limit = { type = officers }
			reduce_pop = 0.99
		}
		diplomatic_influence = { who = FROM value = 25 }
		relation = { who = FROM value = 50 }
		FROM = {
			war_exhaustion = -2.5
			#Add soldiers
			any_pop = {
				limit = { type = soldiers }
				reduce_pop = 1.05
			}
			#Add officers
			any_pop = {
				limit = { type = officers }
				reduce_pop = 1.01
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0.5
			modifier = { factor = 0 war_policy = pacifism }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We will not sacrifice our citizens in a foreign war"
		diplomatic_influence = { who = FROM value = -25 }
		relation = { who = FROM value = -25 }
		FROM = { country_event = 1610104 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.5
			modifier = { factor = 0 war_policy = jingoism }
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = 1610105
	title = "The COVID-19 Virus"
	desc = EVTDESC1610105
	picture = "wuhan_virus_2019"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		year = 2019
		NOT = { year = 2025 }
		owns = 1522
		NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak } }
		any_owned_province = { 
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = dev_1 
				has_province_modifier = dev_2
				has_province_modifier = dev_3
			}
		}
		has_country_flag = sars_outbreak_2003
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 12
	}

	option = {
		name = "Try to cover it up!"
		
		badboy = 3
		
		set_global_flag = covid19_virus_happened
		
		set_global_flag = epidemic_start
		
		set_country_flag = virus_originator_country
		
		set_country_flag = enable_virus_controls
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		
		any_country = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.7 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Do everything we can to stop the outbreak!"

		money = -500000
		
		set_global_flag = covid19_virus_happened

		set_global_flag = epidemic_start
		
		set_country_flag = virus_originator_country
		
		set_country_flag = enable_virus_controls
		
		#Allow virus controls
		any_country = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			country_event = 14120142
		}
		
		set_country_flag = who_alerted_to_new_virus
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		
		any_country = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			add_country_modifier = { name = virus_timer duration = 180 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.3 }
	}

}

		tag = USA
		year = 1994
		NOT = { year = 2000 }

		NOT = { tech_school = XNA_tech_school }

			MEX = { exists = yes is_vassal = no trade_policy = free_trade war = no }
			CAN = { exists = yes is_vassal = no trade_policy = free_trade war = no }
		}
		
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = in_bankrupcy }
		
	}

		months = 1
	}

	}

#Party Split

#Government in Chaos
country_event = {
	id = 1610116
	title = "$COUNTRY_ADJ$ Government in Chaos"
	desc = EVTDESC1610116
	picture = "government_in_chaos"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
	
		#Minority government
		OR = {

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = conservative } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist ruling_party_ideology = conservative } 
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = big_tent }
				ruling_party_ideology = big_tent
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = socialist pop_majority_ideology = communist pop_majority_ideology = communist_social } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social }
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal pop_majority_ideology = progressive } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = progressive }
			}

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = populist } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist }
			}
		
		}
		
		NOT = { publishing_rights = state_publishing }
		
		average_militancy = 5
		average_consciousness = 4
		
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = leadership_chaos
			
			#If there is a party scandal
			has_country_modifier = ruling_party_scandal
			has_country_modifier = party_scandal_evidence 
			
			#Crazy leader
			has_country_modifier = raving_loon
			has_country_modifier = gauche_buffoon
			
			#Leader without control
			has_country_modifier = power_vacuum
		}
		
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = political_strife }
		
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
		modifier = { factor = 3 publishing_rights = censored_publishing }
		modifier = { factor = 2 publishing_rights = responsible_publishing }
	}

	option = {

		prestige_factor = -0.01
		any_pop = { militancy = -3 }
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = political_strife duration = 100 }

			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = conservative } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = big_tent } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = socialist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = traditionalist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = populist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } }

#Fix Egypt being Libya bug
country_event = {
	id = 1610122
	title = "The Libyan State"
	desc = EVTDESC1610122
	picture = "EGY_to_TRI"

	trigger = {
		tag = EGY
		LBY = { exists = no }
		capital_scope = { is_core = LBY }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "This is a state worthy of our lands" 
		
		#Remove stray Egyptian cores in Libya
		all_core = { 
			limit = { is_core = EGY is_core = LBY }
			remove_core = EGY
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { tag = LBY } }
			all_core = { remove_core = LBY }
		}
		
		change_tag = LBY
		
		primary_culture = libyan
		
		EGY = { capital = 1745 primary_culture = egyptian }
	}

}

#Party Hardliners event
country_event = {
	id = 1610123
	title = "Resentful Party Hardliners"
	desc = EVTDESC1610123
	picture = "party_hardliners_revolt"

	trigger = {
		ai = no
		OR = {
			government = presidential_dictatorship
			government = nationalist_dictatorship
			government = sectarian_dictatorship
			government = proletarian_dictatorship
			government = proletarian_dictatorship1
		}
		
		#Adopted some liberalisation
		OR = {
			NOT = { political_opinions = ruling_party_opinion }
			NOT = { political_parties = parties_not_allowed }
			NOT = { vote_franschise = none_voting }
			
			NOT = { OR = { publishing_rights = state_publishing publishing_rights = censored_publishing } }
			
			NOT = { public_meetings = no_meetings }
		}
		
		#Has Conservative officers
		any_pop = {
			type = officers 
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					pop_majority_ideology = liberal
					pop_majority_ideology = progressive
					pop_majority_ideology = populist
					pop_majority_ideology = big_tent
				}
			}
			militancy = 5
		}
		
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6
	}

	option = {
		name = "Accept their request!"
		
		prestige_factor = -0.02
		
		#Party liberals get angry
		any_pop = {
			limit = { type = officers }
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = liberal
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = progressive
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 5
				ideology = populist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 5
				ideology = big_tent
			}
		}
		
		#Party hardliners are happy
		any_pop = {
			limit = { type = officers }
			
			#Moderate blocs
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = -5
				ideology = socialist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = -5
				ideology = conservative
			}
			
			#Extreme blocs
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = -10
				ideology = traditionalist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = -10
				ideology = nationalist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = -10
				ideology = communist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = -10
				ideology = communist_social
			}
		}
		
		#Revert democratic reforms
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					NOT = { OR = { publishing_rights = state_publishing publishing_rights = censored_publishing } }
				} 
			}
			owner = { political_reform = state_publishing }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					NOT = { public_meetings = no_meetings }
				} 
			}
			owner = { political_reform = no_meetings }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					NOT = { political_opinions = ruling_party_opinion } 
				} 
			}
			owner = { political_reform = ruling_party_opinion }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					NOT = { political_parties = parties_not_allowed }
				} 
			}
			owner = { political_reform = parties_not_allowed }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					NOT = { vote_franschise = none_voting }
				} 
			}
			owner = { political_reform = none_voting }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.6 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "I am the $MONARCHTITLE$, I do what I want"
		
		#Party hardliners are angry
		any_pop = {
			limit = { type = officers }
			
			#Moderate blocs
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 5
				ideology = socialist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 5
				ideology = conservative
			}
			
			#Extreme blocs
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = traditionalist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = nationalist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = communist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = communist_social
			}
		}
		
		#If military loyalty is not low
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = military_loyalty_low } } 
			}
			owner = {
				random = {
					chance = 15
					country_event = 1610049
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					country_event = 1210202
				}
			}
		}
		
		#If military loyalty is low
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { has_country_modifier = military_loyalty_low } 
			}
			owner = {
				country_event = 100100 #Coup Risk
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.4 }
	}

}

#Gibraltar SAR
country_event = {
	id = 1610126
	title = "Gibraltar Constitution Order $YEAR$"
	desc = EVTDESC1610126
	picture = "GIB_SAR_ENG"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		year = 2006
		
		OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 government = democracy government = democracy1 }
		NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
		
		war = no
		is_vassal = no
		
		#Owns Gibraltar
		is_possible_vassal = GIB
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 11
	}

	option = {
		name = "Grant Gibraltar full internal autonomy"
		prestige_factor = 0.01
		release_vassal = GIB
		GIB = { government = sar_government country_event = 800054 ruling_party_ideology = conservative }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = GIB value = 200 }
		
		relation = { who = SPA value = 50 }
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.8 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Keep Gibraltar an integral part of the nation"
		badboy = 5
		
		#Nationalist pops are not happy
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_core = GIB }
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = populist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = nationalist
			}
		}
		
		relation = { who = SPA value = -50 }
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.2 }
	}

}

#Rapid capitulation by the AI
country_event = {
	id = 1610129
	title = "$COUNTRY_ADJ$ Unconditional Surrender"
	desc = EVTDESC1610129
	picture = "remove_all_bourgeoisie"
	
	major = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		
		war = yes
		
		is_vassal = no
		
		#Capital is occupied by the enemy
		capital_scope = {
			NOT = { controlled_by = THIS } 
			controlled_by_rebels = no
		}
		
		#Situation is grim
		OR = {
			AND = { national_provinces_occupied = 0.50 war_policy = pacifism }
			AND = { national_provinces_occupied = 0.75 war_policy = pro_military }
		}
		
		#Not jingoism
		NOT = { war_policy = jingoism }
		
		#THIS army has been defeated
		NOT = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
		
		#Not when the cold war is hot
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = cold_war_hot }
		
		#Not already surrended
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nation_has_capitulated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = "The $COUNTRY_ADJ$ nation has been defeated"
		
		set_country_flag = nation_has_capitulated
		
		#Surrender to a country we are at war with
		random_country = {
			limit = { war_with = THIS }
			country_event = 1610130
		}
		
		#Nationalists are furious!
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } }
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = nationalist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = populist
			}
		}
	}

}

#Rapid capitulation by the AI
country_event = {
	id = 1610130
	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Unconditional Surrender"
	desc = EVTDESC1610130
	picture = "ai_quick_capitulation"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "Is end of the war near?"
		
		FROM = {
			any_owned = { 
				limit = { controlled_by = FROM } 
				change_controller = THIS
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }

	}
	
	option = {
		name = "They shall pay for the war!"
		
		badboy = 3
		
		FROM = {
			any_owned = { 
				limit = { controlled_by = FROM } 
				change_controller = THIS
				owner = { THIS = { money = 5000 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = war_bombed duration = 1825 }
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }

	}

}

#Clean up UNO tag
country_event = {
	id = 1610131
	title = "The United Nations"
	desc = EVTDESC1610131
	picture = "united_nations"

	trigger = {
		UNO = { exists = yes }
		any_neighbor_country = { tag = UNO }
	}

		name = "The UN is now being operated from $COUNTRY_ADJ$ territory"
		prestige = 50
		inherit = UNO
	}

}

#USSR overthrow the reformists
country_event = {
	id = 1610132
	title = "Coup by the Soviet Hardliners?"
	desc = EVTDESC1610132
	picture = "soviet_coup_no_reformists"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		
		OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 }
		war = yes
		is_vassal = no
		
		ruling_party_ideology = communist_social
		war_policy = pacifism
		
		#Must be losing the war
		national_provinces_occupied = 0.10
		
		#THIS is not an aggressor
		NOT = { has_country_flag = this_is_aggressor }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Remove the pacifists!"
		
		#Switch to hardliners
		ruling_party_ideology = communist
		
		#Purge the government
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { OR = { type = officers type = bureaucrats type = aristocrats } } 
			reduce_pop = 0.90
			ideology = { factor = 0.25 value = communist } 
			dominant_issue = {
				value = jingoism
				factor = 0.25
			}
		}
		
		#Middle class is pissed
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { NOT = { type = bureaucrats } strata = middle } 
			militancy = 5
			ideology = { factor = 0.25 value = liberal } 
		}
		
		#Lower class doesn't really care
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { NOT = { type = soldiers } strata = poor } 
			militancy = 1
			ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = liberal } 
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "The coup fails"
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = political_strife duration = 365 }
		
		#Hardliners are furious
		any_pop = {
			limit = { OR = { type = officers type = bureaucrats type = aristocrats } } 
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = communist
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				value = jingoism
				factor = 0.25
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}

#Dictatorship after a nuclear strike
country_event = {
	id = 1610133
	title = "The Continuity of Government"
	desc = EVTDESC1610133
	picture = "post_nuke_cog"

	trigger = {
	
		#Democratic government
		OR = {
			government = democracy
			government = democracy1
			
			government = hms_government
			government = hms_government1
			
			government = socialist_democracy
		}
		
		is_vassal = no
	
		#Country has been hit by nuclear weapons
		any_owned_province = { 
			OR = { 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_high 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_medium 
				has_province_modifier = nuke_low 
			} 
		}
		
		#Has some proper Civil Defence
		OR = { 
			has_country_modifier = cdhigh 
			has_country_modifier = cdmedium 
		}
		
		#Civil Defence shelters activated
		has_country_flag = nuke_protection
		
		NOT = { has_country_flag = post_nuke_government }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 0.1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Grant the regional administrators absolute power"
		
		set_country_flag = post_nuke_government
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } } }
			owner = { government = absolute_monarchy }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 } } }
			owner = { government = presidential_dictatorship }
		}
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { government = socialist_democracy } }
			owner = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
		}
		
		#Set dictatorial reform
		political_reform = none_voting 
		political_reform = ruling_party_opinion
		political_reform = no_meetings
		political_reform = politicised_service
		political_reform = state_publishing
		political_reform = no_trade_unions
		political_reform = parties_not_allowed
		political_reform = open_immigration
		political_reform = mandatory_service
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Try to preserve the pre-war order"
		
		set_country_flag = post_nuke_government
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = political_strife duration = 3650 }
		
		any_owned = {
			add_province_modifier = { name = generic_uprising duration = 730 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

}

#Five Year Plan - Economic Specialisation
country_event = {
	id = 1610134
	title = "The Five Year Plan of $YEAR$"
	desc = EVTDESC1610134
	picture = "five_year_plan_choice"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "Focus on Heavy Industry"
		add_country_modifier = { name = spclow duration = -1 }
		
		set_country_flag = spclow
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.6 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Focus on Consumer Goods"
		add_country_modifier = { name = spcmedium duration = -1 }
		
		set_country_flag = spcmedium

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.2 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Focus on Services"
		add_country_modifier = { name = spchigh duration = -1 }
		
		set_country_flag = spchigh
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Focus on Military Production"
		add_country_modifier = { name = spcno duration = -1 }
		
		set_country_flag = spcno
		
		#Military is happy
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = nationalist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = traditionalist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = conservative } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = liberal } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = big_tent } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = progressive } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = socialist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist_social } } } }
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}

#Gridlocked Legislature - start
country_event = {
	id = 1610135
	title = "Gridlocked Legislature"
	desc = EVTDESC1610135
	picture = "gridlocked_legislature"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = gridlocked_legislature }
		
		OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
		
		#Only affects Presidential and Semi-Presidential systems
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = presidential_system_republic
			has_country_flag = semi_presidential_system_republic
		}

		OR = { 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = conservative } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist ruling_party_ideology = conservative } 
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = big_tent }
				ruling_party_ideology = big_tent
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = socialist pop_majority_ideology = communist pop_majority_ideology = communist_social } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social }
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal pop_majority_ideology = progressive } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = progressive }
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = populist } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist }
			} 

		}
		
		
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 24 #roughly coincide with midterms for democracies
	}

	option = {
		name = "The $MONARCHTITLE$'s hands must not be tied!"
		set_country_flag = gridlocked_legislature
		
		any_pop = {
			limit = { location = { is_colonial = no } }
			militancy = 1
			consciousness = 1
		}
		
	}

}

#Gridlocked Legislature - end
country_event = {
	id = 1610136
	title = "Gridlock in Legislature Cleared"
	desc = EVTDESC1610136
	picture = "gridlocked_legislature_cleared"

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = gridlocked_legislature
		
		OR = {
			
			#Exempted gov type
			NOT = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy } }
		
			#Parliamentary Republic
			has_country_flag = parliamentary_system_republic

			#Ruling party is once again a majority party
			AND = { 
				OR = { pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = conservative }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist ruling_party_ideology = conservative } 
			} 

			AND = { 
				pop_majority_ideology = big_tent
				ruling_party_ideology = big_tent
			} 

			AND = { 
				OR = { pop_majority_ideology = socialist pop_majority_ideology = communist pop_majority_ideology = communist_social }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social }
			} 

			AND = { 
				OR = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal pop_majority_ideology = progressive }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = progressive }
			} 

			AND = { 
				OR = { pop_majority_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = populist }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist }
			} 

		}
		
		
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			NOT = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "I still need more power!"
		clr_country_flag = gridlocked_legislature
		
		any_pop = {
			limit = { location = { is_colonial = no } }
			militancy = -1
			consciousness = -1
		}
		
	}

}

#Fall of the United Kingdom
country_event = {
	id = 1610142
	title = "Fall of $COUNTRY$"
	desc = "EVTDESC1610142"
	picture = "notre_dame_fire"
	
	major = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		
		#Does not own London
		NOT = { owns = 300 }
		
		is_vassal = no
		war = no
		
		exists = ENL
	}

	option = {
		name = "The $COUNTRY_ADJ$ nation is but just a footnote in history."
		inherit = ENL
		capital = 300
		change_tag = ENL
		
		primary_culture = british
		remove_accepted_culture = scottish
		remove_accepted_culture = welsh
		
		#Clean up
		ENG = {
			primary_culture = british
			add_accepted_culture = scottish
			add_accepted_culture = welsh
		}
	}

}

#Expelled from Military Alliance
country_event = {
	id = 1610143
	title = "Expelled from Global Military Alliance"
	desc = "EVTDESC1610143"
	picture = "expelled_from_global_alliance"

	trigger = {
		
		#Not NATO Leader
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = nato_leader }
		
		#Not bloc leader
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = communist_bloc_leader }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = democratic_bloc_leader }
		
		#Part of a global bloc
		OR = {
			AND = { has_country_modifier = alliance_nato THIS = { has_country_modifier = alliance_nato } }
			AND = { has_country_modifier = rio_pact THIS = { has_country_modifier = rio_pact } }	
			AND = { has_country_modifier = warsaw_pact THIS = { has_country_modifier = warsaw_pact } }
			AND = { has_country_modifier = csto_alliance THIS = { has_country_modifier = csto_alliance } }	
			AND = { has_country_modifier = anzus_alliance THIS = { has_country_modifier = anzus_alliance } }
			AND = { has_country_modifier = sco_pact THIS = { has_country_modifier = sco_pact } }
			AND = { has_country_modifier = cento_member THIS = { has_country_modifier = cento_member } }
		}
		
		#THIS is a pariah
		has_country_modifier = international_pariah
		badboy = 1
		
		#THIS is independent
		is_vassal = no
		
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10
		modifier = { factor = 0.1 has_country_modifier = cold_war_high }
		modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_modifier = cold_war_medium }
		
		modifier = { factor = 0.1 has_country_modifier = world_high }
		modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_modifier = world_medium }
	}

	option = {
		name = "They 'wish' us well"
		
		any_pop = { militancy = 1 consciousness = 2 }
		
		#NATO
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = alliance_nato } }
			owner = {
				prestige_factor = -0.01
				remove_country_modifier = alliance_nato
				
				add_country_modifier = { name = leave_alliance_nato duration = 1825 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = alliance_nato } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } leave_alliance = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		#Rio Pact
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = rio_pact } }
			owner = {
				prestige_factor = -0.01
				remove_country_modifier = rio_pact
				
				add_country_modifier = { name = leave_rio_pact duration = 1825 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = rio_pact } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } leave_alliance = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		#Warsaw Pact
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = warsaw_pact } }
			owner = {
				prestige_factor = -0.01
				remove_country_modifier = warsaw_pact
				
				add_country_modifier = { name = leave_warsaw_pact duration = 1825 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = warsaw_pact } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } leave_alliance = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		#CSTO
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = csto_alliance } }
			owner = {
				prestige_factor = -0.01
				remove_country_modifier = csto_alliance
				
				add_country_modifier = { name = leave_csto_alliance duration = 1825 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = csto_alliance } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } leave_alliance = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		#ANZUS
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = anzus_alliance } }
			owner = {
				prestige_factor = -0.01
				remove_country_modifier = anzus_alliance
				
				add_country_modifier = { name = leave_anzus_alliance duration = 1825 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = anzus_alliance } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } leave_alliance = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		#SCO Pact
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = sco_pact } }
			owner = {
				prestige_factor = -0.01
				remove_country_modifier = sco_pact
				
				add_country_modifier = { name = leave_sco_pact duration = 1825 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = sco_pact } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } leave_alliance = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		#CENTO Pact
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = cento_member } }
			owner = {
				prestige_factor = -0.01
				remove_country_modifier = cento_member

				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = cento_member } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } leave_alliance = THIS }

		tag = TRB
		
		is_vassal = no

		OR = {
			TRE = { exists = yes }
			YUG = { exists = yes }
			SLO = { exists = yes }
			ITA = { exists = yes }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Get annexed"
		
		#Inherit in order of priority
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { TRE = { exists = yes } } } owner = { TRE = { prestige = 50 inherit = TRB } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { TRE = { exists = no } YUG = { exists = yes } } } owner = { YUG = { prestige = 50 inherit = TRB } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { TRE = { exists = no } YUG = { exists = no } SLO = { exists = yes } } } owner = { SLO = { prestige = 50 inherit = TRB } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { TRE = { exists = no } YUG = { exists = no } SLO = { exists = no } ITA = { exists = yes } } } owner = { ITA = { prestige = 50 inherit = TRB } } }
		
		TRB = { all_core = { remove_core = TRB } }

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Remain independent!"
		money = -25000
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}

			government = democracy1

			ruling_party_ideology = nationalist
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}

		name = "It is war then!"
		badboy = 5

		GAG = {
			government = democracy1
			country_event = 800054
			ruling_party_ideology = nationalist
		}

				defender_goal = { } 
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}
