#Union Event
country_event = {
	id = 1610151
	title = "Union with Cultural Union?"
	desc = EVTDESC1610151
	picture = "cultural_union_annexation"

	#fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		#THIS is a product of an unnatural partition
		OR = { 
			has_country_flag = great_war_mandate_un 
			has_country_flag = unnatural_partition_of_country 
		}
		
		is_vassal = no
		war = no
		
		election = no
	
		#THIS is not a cultural union
		is_cultural_union = no
		
		#A neighbouring country is a GP or SP and is the cultural union of THIS and shares the same gov type as THIS and has good relations with THIS
		any_neighbor_country = { 
			is_cultural_union = THIS 
			
			OR = { 
				is_greater_power = yes 
				is_secondary_power = yes 
			}
			is_vassal = no
			war = no
			
			relation = { who = THIS value = 100 }
			
			OR = {
				#Republican democracy grouping
				AND = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 } } }
				
				#Monarchy democracy grouping
				AND = { OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } THIS = { OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } } }
				
				#Communist dictatorship grouping
				AND = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } } }
				
				#Monarchy dictatorship grouping
				AND = { government = absolute_monarchy THIS = { government = absolute_monarchy } }
				
				#Theocratic dictatorship grouping
				AND = { government = theocracy THIS = { government = theocracy } }
				
				#Socialist Republic grouping
				AND = { government = socialist_democracy THIS = { government = socialist_democracy } }
			}
		}
		
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 12
	}

	option = {
		name = "Join our cultural kin!"
		
		clr_country_flag = great_war_mandate_un 
		clr_country_flag = unnatural_partition_of_country 
		
		#Cultural Union annexes THIS
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_cultural_union = THIS 
				
				OR = { 
					is_greater_power = yes 
					is_secondary_power = yes 
				}
				is_vassal = no 
				war = no
				
				neighbour = THIS
				
				relation = { who = THIS value = 100 }
				
				OR = {
					#Republican democracy grouping
					AND = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 } } }
				
					#Monarchy democracy grouping
					AND = { OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } THIS = { OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } } }
				
					#Communist dictatorship grouping
					AND = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } } }
				
					#Monarchy dictatorship grouping
					AND = { government = absolute_monarchy THIS = { government = absolute_monarchy } }
				
					#Theocratic dictatorship grouping
					AND = { government = theocracy THIS = { government = theocracy } }
				
					#Socialist Republic grouping
					AND = { government = socialist_democracy THIS = { government = socialist_democracy } }
				}
			}
			
			country_event = 11107
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "$COUNTRY_ADJ$ sovereignty is sacred!"
		prestige = 100
		
		clr_country_flag = great_war_mandate_un 
		clr_country_flag = unnatural_partition_of_country 
		
		#Cultural Union loses relation with THIS
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_cultural_union = THIS 
				
				OR = { 
					is_greater_power = yes 
					is_secondary_power = yes 
				}
				is_vassal = no 
				war = no
				
				neighbour = THIS
				
				relation = { who = THIS value = 100 }
				
				OR = {
					#Republican democracy grouping
					AND = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 } } }
				
					#Monarchy democracy grouping
					AND = { OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } THIS = { OR = { government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } } }
				
					#Communist dictatorship grouping
					AND = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } } }
				
					#Monarchy dictatorship grouping
					AND = { government = absolute_monarchy THIS = { government = absolute_monarchy } }
				
					#Theocratic dictatorship grouping
					AND = { government = theocracy THIS = { government = theocracy } }
				
					#Socialist Republic grouping
					AND = { government = socialist_democracy THIS = { government = socialist_democracy } }
				}
			}
			
			relation = { who = THIS value = -100 }
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -100 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

}

	title = "Chairmanship of the IBRD"
	desc = "The Chairmanship of the IBRD is rotating again. The Chairmanship only lasts 5 years." 
	picture = "world_bank"
	
	trigger = {
		year = 1946
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = ibrd_chairmanship }
		has_country_flag = ibrd_chairmanship
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We had a good run."
		random_country = { limit = { AND = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = ibrd_chairmanship } has_country_modifier = ibrd_member has_country_modifier = creditor_nation } } country_event = 1300022 }
		remove_country_modifier = ibrd_chairmanship
		clr_country_flag = ibrd_chairmanship
	}
}

#Rotating Chairmanship of the IBRD - select the new leader
country_event = {
	id = 1300022
	title = "Chairmanship of the IBRD"
	desc = "The Chairmanship of the IBRD is rotating and the Chairmanship has come to us. The Chairmanship only lasts 5 years." 
	picture = "world_bank"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Splendid!"
		prestige = 10
		add_country_modifier = { name = ibrd_chairmanship duration = 1825 }
		set_country_flag = ibrd_chairmanship
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = ibrd_chairmanship remove_country_modifier = ibrd_chairmanship } #Just in case
	}
}

#Rotating Chairmanships USA first - IBRD
country_event = {
	id = 1300025
	title = "Chairmanship of the IBRD"
	desc = "The Chairmanship of the IBRD is currently vacant so we have been chosen to fill it. The Chairmanship only lasts 5 years." 
	picture = "world_bank"
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		is_greater_power = yes
		has_country_modifier = ibrd_member
		#NOT = { has_global_flag = ibrdusafirst }
		
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = ibrd_chairmanship }
		
		NOT = { any_greater_power = { has_country_modifier = ibrd_chairmanship } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	option = {
		name = "Splendid!"
		prestige = 10
		add_country_modifier = { name = ibrd_chairmanship duration = 1825 }
		set_country_flag = ibrd_chairmanship
		set_global_flag = ibrdusafirst

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { OR = { economic_policy = state_capitalism economic_policy = planned_economy1 economic_policy = planned_economy } } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = ibrdhigh_gp duration = -1 } 
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = ibrd_member } add_country_modifier = { name = ibrdhigh duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { economic_policy = interventionism } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = ibrdmedium_gp duration = -1 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = ibrd_member } add_country_modifier = { name = ibrdmedium duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { economic_policy = laissez_faire } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = ibrdlow_gp duration = -1 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = ibrd_member } add_country_modifier = { name = ibrdlow duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		
	}
	
}

#Rotating Chairmanships USA first - IMF
country_event = {
	id = 1300023
	title = "Chairmanship of the IMF"

	picture = "world_bank"
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_greater_power = yes
		has_country_modifier = imf_member
		#NOT = { has_global_flag = imfusafirst }
		
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = imf_chairmanship }
		
		NOT = { any_greater_power = { has_country_modifier = imf_chairmanship } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	option = {
		name = "Splendid!"
		prestige = 10
		add_country_modifier = { name = imf_chairmanship duration = 1825 }
		set_country_flag = imf_chairmanship
		set_global_flag = imfusafirst
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { OR = { economic_policy = state_capitalism economic_policy = planned_economy1 economic_policy = planned_economy } } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = imfhigh duration = -1 } 
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = imf_member } add_country_modifier = { name = imfhigh duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { economic_policy = interventionism } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = imfmedium duration = -1 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = imf_member } add_country_modifier = { name = imfmedium duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { economic_policy = laissez_faire } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = imflow duration = -1 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = imf_member } add_country_modifier = { name = imflow duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		
	}
	
}
#Rotating Chairmanships USA first - WTO
country_event = {
	id = 1300024
	title = "Chairmanship of the WTO"
	desc = "The Chairmanship of the WTO is currently vacant so we have been chosen to fill it. The Chairmanship only lasts 5 years." 
	picture = "world_bank"
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		is_greater_power = yes
		has_country_modifier = wto_member
		#NOT = { has_global_flag = wtousafirst }
		
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = wto_chairmanship }
		
		NOT = { any_greater_power = { has_country_modifier = wto_chairmanship } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	option = {
		name = "Splendid!"
		prestige = 10
		add_country_modifier = { name = wto_chairmanship duration = 1825 }
		set_country_flag = wto_chairmanship
		set_global_flag = wtousafirst
		set_global_flag = wto_created
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { trade_policy = protectionism } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = wtohigh duration = -1 } 
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = wto_member } add_country_modifier = { name = wtohigh duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { trade_policy = free_trade NOT = { economic_policy = laissez_faire } } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = wtomedium duration = -1 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = wto_member } add_country_modifier = { name = wtomedium duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { trade_policy = free_trade economic_policy = laissez_faire } } 
			owner = { 
				add_country_modifier = { name = wtolow duration = -1 }
				any_country = { limit = { has_country_modifier = wto_member } add_country_modifier = { name = wtolow duration = -1 } }
			} 
		}
		
	}
	
}
#Decolonisation remove techschool
country_event = {
	id = 1300027
	title = "Decline of the $COUNTRY_ADJ$ Empire"
	desc = EVT_15403_DESC
	picture = "colonialism_self_rule"

	trigger = {

		NOT = { year = 1990 }

		OR = { 
AND = { 
tag = POR
war = no
OR = { is_vassal = yes is_greater_power = no }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = ANG } NOT = { owns = 1999 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = MOZ } NOT = { owns = 2049 }
}

AND = { 
tag = ENG
war = no
OR = { is_vassal = yes is_greater_power = no }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = RAJ } NOT = { owns = 1236 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = HND } NOT = { owns = 1236 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = NGE } NOT = { owns = 1941 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = SUD } NOT = { owns = 1827 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = TAN } NOT = { owns = 2036 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = FMS } NOT = { owns = 1387 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = MSY } NOT = { owns = 1387 }
}

AND = { 
tag = FRA
war = no
OR = { is_vassal = yes is_greater_power = no }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = ALG } NOT = { owns = 1700 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = CAR } NOT = { owns = 1965 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = IVC } NOT = { owns = 1892 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = MAD } NOT = { owns = 2115 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = MLI } NOT = { owns = 1794 }
}

AND = { 
tag = SPA
war = no
OR = { is_vassal = yes is_greater_power = no }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = WSA } NOT = { owns = 1773 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = EQG } NOT = { owns = 1955 }
}

AND = { 
tag = FBU
war = no
OR = { is_vassal = yes is_greater_power = no }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = RAJ } NOT = { owns = 1236 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = HND } NOT = { owns = 1236 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = NGE } NOT = { owns = 1941 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = SUD } NOT = { owns = 1827 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = TAN } NOT = { owns = 2036 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = FMS } NOT = { owns = 1387 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = MSY } NOT = { owns = 1387 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = ALG } NOT = { owns = 1700 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = CAR } NOT = { owns = 1965 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = IVC } NOT = { owns = 1892 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = MAD } NOT = { owns = 2115 }
NOT = { is_our_vassal = MLI } NOT = { owns = 1794 }
}

		}

		NOT = { has_country_flag = decoloniasation2 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }

	option = {
		name = "Au revoir $COUNTRY_ADJ$ imperialism!"
		prestige_factor = -0.05 
		badboy = -5
		set_country_flag = decoloniasation2
		}

}

#SAR status
country_event = {
	id = 1300029
	title = "Special Administrative Region Status"
	desc = "$COUNTRY$'s Special Administrative Status only lasts for 50 years before we revert to direct rule by China."
	picture = "nwo2_chinese_hongkong"

	trigger = {
		OR = { tag = HKG tag = MCA }
		is_vassal_of = CHI
		government = sar_government
		NOT = { has_country_flag = endofsarstatus }

	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Noted"
		add_country_modifier = { name = sar_status duration = 18250 }
		set_country_flag = endofsarstatus
		}
	}
#End of SAR status
country_event = {
	id = 1300030
	title = "Special Administrative Region Status"
	desc = "$COUNTRY$'s Special Administrative Status has ended so we revert to direct rule by China."
	picture = "macao"

	trigger = {
		OR = { tag = HKG tag = MCA }
		exists = CHI
		is_vassal_of = CHI
		year = 2040
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = sar_status }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = endofsarstatus1 }

	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Noted"
	    CHI = { inherit = THIS }
		set_country_flag = endofsarstatus1
	}
}
	
#End of SAR status
country_event = {
	id = 1300031
	title = "Special Administrative Region Status"
	desc = "$COUNTRY$'s Special Administrative Status has ended because we are now independent."
	picture = "macao"

	trigger = {
		
		NOT = { OR = { tag = IAR tag = TRE tag = DZG tag = SCS tag = UNT tag = TGZ tag = JRU tag = ICB } }
		
		is_vassal = no
		
		government = sar_government
		NOT = { has_country_flag = endofsarstatus2 }

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 3 }
	
	option = {
		name = "Rejoice!"
		government = democracy
		remove_country_modifier = sar_status
		set_country_flag = endofsarstatus2
	}
}

	desc = "With the loss of our empire, our capital can no longer be classified as an imperial capital."
	picture = "imperialcapital"

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = decoloniasation2

		}

	name = "We need to find a new role for our capital!"

		set_country_flag = impcapital
		}

	}

#Kick out of OPEC
country_event = {
	id = 1400013
	title = "Expelled from OPEC"
	desc = "The OPEC Council has deemed our membership as invalid due to 1. Either we are a vassal or 2. We do not produce oil anymore or 3. Our gov type is incompatible."
	picture = "kickedoutofopec"

	trigger = {
		has_country_modifier = opecmember
		OR = { 
			NOT = { any_owned_province = { trade_goods = petroleum } } 
			is_vassal = yes 
			government = proletarian_dictatorship 
			government = proletarian_dictatorship1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We can go it alone!"
		prestige = -10
		
		remove_country_modifier = opecmember
		any_owned = { 
			remove_province_modifier = oil_high 
			remove_province_modifier = oil_medium 
			remove_province_modifier = oil_low 
		}
		clr_country_flag = oil_high
		clr_country_flag = oil_medium
		clr_country_flag = oil_low
	}
	
}
#Vietnamese Doi Moi
country_event = {
	id = 1400014
	title = "Doi Moi"
	desc = EVTDESC1400014
	picture = "doimoi"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = DAI
		
		#1980s onwards
		neoliberalism = 1
		
		war = no
		is_vassal = no
		
		ruling_party_ideology = communist
		OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 }
		
		OR = { 
			NOT = { has_global_flag = blocsenabled } 
			market_communism = 1
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }

	option = {
		name = "Begin the reforms!"
		prestige = 10
		ruling_party_ideology = communist_social
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Stick it to the old ways!"
		prestige = -20
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}
}

	id = 1400015

	desc = EVTDESC1400015
	picture = "chinesemarketreforms"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		
		#1980s onwards
		neoliberalism = 1
		
		war = no
		is_vassal = no
		
		ruling_party_ideology = communist
		OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 }
		
		OR = { 
			NOT = { has_global_flag = blocsenabled } 
			market_communism = 1
		}
		
		#Different chain for Deng
		NOT = { has_country_flag = deng_xiaoping_selected }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	option = {
		name = "Begin the reforms!"
		prestige = 500
		ruling_party_ideology = communist_social
		clr_country_flag = economic_malaise
		set_country_flag = industrious_nation
		add_country_modifier = { name = economic_boom duration = 3650 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Stop the reforms!"
		prestige = -100
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}
}

	trigger = {
has_country_flag = disabled_for_now

NOT = { has_country_flag = unite_yemen }

YEM = { is_vassal = no war = no }
SYE = { is_vassal = no war = no }

RUS = { NOT = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } } }
YEM = { NOT = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } } }	
		}

mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	option = {
	name = "Unite the Yemeni people!"
		prestige = 20
		inherit = SYE
		set_country_flag = unite_yemen
			}

	option = {
	name = "Form a federation!"
		prestige = 20
		inherit = SYE
		set_country_flag = unite_yemen
			}

		}

#Central African Empire initiation
country_event = {
	id = 1400024
	title = "Coup in the Central African Republic?"
	desc = EVTDESC1400024
	picture = "carcoup"
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAR
		year = 1966
		NOT = { year = 1990 }
		government = democracy
		is_vassal = no
		war = no
	}

	option = {
		name = "Launch the coup!"
		government = presidential_dictatorship
		country_event = 800050
		ruling_party_ideology = nationalist
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "Keep the unstable democracy!"
		add_country_modifier = { name = revolution_chaos duration = 1825 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}

#Central African Empire
country_event = {
	id = 1400025
	title = "Central African Empire"
	desc = EVTDESC1400025
	picture = "cae"
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CAR
		year = 1976
		NOT = { year = 1990 }
		
		government = presidential_dictatorship
		war = no
		is_vassal = no
		
		OR = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist ruling_party_ideology = nationalist }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Become a monarchy!"
		government = absolute_monarchy
		prestige = 100
		add_country_modifier = { name = revolution_chaos duration = 1825 }
		any_pop = { militancy = 5 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Being President for Life is good enough!"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}

		}

	}

			limit = { owner = { FROM = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } }
			owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { FROM = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } }
			owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive }
		}
		
		political_reform = free_voting
		political_reform = semi_democratic_state_opinion
		political_reform = limited_meetings
		political_reform = elitist_service
		political_reform = responsible_publishing
		political_reform = state_controlled_unions
		political_reform = parties_restricted
		political_reform = jefferson_method
		
		#Domestic reaction
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { strata = rich }
			militancy = 10
			consciousness = 10
			ideology = { factor = 0.25 value = communist }
		}
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { strata = middle }
			militancy = -5
			consciousness = -5
			ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = progressive }
		}
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { strata = middle }
			militancy = -2.5
			consciousness = -2.5
			ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = socialist }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We shall go our own way!"
		
		#USS loses influence in THIS
		overlord = { 
			relation = { who = THIS value = -200 }
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -100 }
			release_vassal = THIS 
		}
		
		#Domestic reaction
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { strata = rich }
			militancy = -5
			consciousness = -5
		}
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { strata = middle }
			militancy = 6
			consciousness = 6
			ideology = { factor = 0.2 value = liberal }
		}
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { strata = middle }
			militancy = 3
			consciousness = 3
			ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = liberal }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}
	
}

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { FROM = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } } owner = { any_pop = { militancy = 2 consciousness = 1 ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = socialist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { FROM = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } } owner = { any_pop = { militancy = 2 consciousness = 1 ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = communist } } } }

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { FROM = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { militancy = 2 consciousness = 1 ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = nationalist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { FROM = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } } owner = { any_pop = { militancy = 2 consciousness = 1 ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = populist } } } }

		random_country = {

				literacy = 0.04
			}
		}
	}

#Gurkha Treaty
country_event = {
	id = 1410173
	title = "Tripartite Agreement"
	desc = EVTDESC1410173
	picture = "tripartite_agreement"
	
	trigger = {
		OR = { tag = HND tag = ENG }
		NOT = { exists = RAJ }
		NOT = { war_with = HND }
		NOT = { war_with = NEP }
		NOT = { war_with = ENG }
		HND = { is_vassal = no }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = tripartite_agreement }
		ENG = { is_greater_power = yes }
		year = 1947
		NOT = { year = 1990 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 4
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Sign the Agreement"
		money = -100000
		NEP = { money = 100000 }
		set_country_flag = tripartite_agreement
		set_country_flag = has_mercenary_training
		
		#India accepts nepali
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { tag = HND } }
			owner = { add_accepted_culture = nepali }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Abandon the Agreement"
		set_country_flag = tripartite_agreement
		prestige = -5
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

}

#Deforestation level 1
country_event = {
	id = 1410174
	title = "Light deforestation"
	desc = EVTDESC1410174
	picture = "deforestation"
	
	
	trigger = {

OR = { year = 1980 has_country_flag = unlock_the_amazon }

NOT = { has_country_flag = deforestation1 }

NOT = { has_country_flag = deforestation2 }

NOT = { has_country_flag = deforestation3 }

NOT = { has_country_flag = deforestation4 }

NOT = { has_country_flag = deforestation5 }

any_owned_province = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = deforestation2 } }

any_owned_province = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = deforestation3 } }

any_owned_province = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = deforestation4 } }

any_owned_province = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = deforestation5 } }

any_owned_province = { trade_goods = timber }

any_owned_province = { trade_goods = timber NOT = { has_province_modifier = deforestation1 } }
				}

mean_time_to_happen = { 
months = 120
modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = unlock_the_amazon }
}
	
	option = {
	name = "A loss to $COUNTRY$'s biodiversity"
any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = deforestation1 }
any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = deforestation2 }
any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = deforestation3 }
any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = deforestation4 }
any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = deforestation5 }
set_country_flag = deforestation1
any_owned = { limit = { OR = { trade_goods = timber trade_goods = lumber } } add_province_modifier = { name = deforestation1 duration = -1 } }
		}
}

	desc = "Due to the changing nature of our current conflict with our enemies, the Anti-War Movement has re-evaluated their stance and has decided that it is no longer in the National Interest to continue the Movement."

	trigger = {
		OR = { war = no national_provinces_occupied = 0.25 }

	}

#Microstates - AI only
country_event = {
	id = 1412041
	title = "Microstates"
	desc = "There are many interesting microstates throughout the world."
	picture = "rising_sea_level"

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		
		#Event does not fire for the country that owns the Microstate
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				owns = 603 
				owns = 472
				owns = 457
				owns = 749
				owns = 743
			} 
		}
		
		#Province modifier representing the microstates does not exist and the microstate was not annexed
		OR = { 
			AND = { 603 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = liechenstein } } NOT = { has_global_flag = liechenstein_annexed_flag } }
			AND = { 472 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = monaco } } NOT = { has_global_flag = monaco_annexed_flag } }
			AND = { 457 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = andorra } } NOT = { has_global_flag = andorra_annexed_flag } }
			AND = { 749 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = vatican_city } } NOT = { has_global_flag = vatican_city_annexed_flag } }
			AND = { 743 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = san_marino } } NOT = { has_global_flag = san_marino_annexed_flag } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Interesting Microstates"
		
		random_country = { limit = { owns = 603 603 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = liechenstein } } NOT = { has_global_flag = liechenstein_annexed_flag } } 603 = { add_province_modifier = { name = liechenstein duration = -1 } } }
		random_country = { limit = { owns = 472 472 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = monaco } } NOT = { has_global_flag = monaco_annexed_flag } } 472 = { add_province_modifier = { name = monaco duration = -1 } } }
		random_country = { limit = { owns = 457 457 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = andorra } } NOT = { has_global_flag = andorra_annexed_flag } } 457 = { add_province_modifier = { name = andorra duration = -1 } } }
		random_country = { limit = { owns = 749 749 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = vatican_city } } NOT = { has_global_flag = vatican_city_annexed_flag } } 749 = { add_province_modifier = { name = vatican_city duration = -1 } } }
		random_country = { limit = { owns = 743 743 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = san_marino } } NOT = { has_global_flag = san_marino_annexed_flag } } 743 = { add_province_modifier = { name = san_marino duration = -1 } } }

	}

}

#Uniting for Peace Secondary Powers Recipients
country_event = {
	id = 1412042
	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ invokes Uniting for Peace"
	desc = EVTDESC1412042
	picture = "uniting_for_peace"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Vote in favour of $FROMCOUNTRY$!"
		relation = { who = FROM value = 20 }
		any_country = { 
			limit = { 
				is_vassal = no 
				war_with = FROM 
			} 
			country_event = 1412043 
		}

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				NOT = { relation = { who = FROM value = 100 } } 
			} 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Vote against $FROMCOUNTRY$!"
		relation = { who = FROM value = -20 }
		any_country = { 
			limit = { war_with = FROM } 
			relation = { who = THIS value = 10 } 
		}

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				relation = { who = FROM value = 100 } 
			} 
		}
	}

}

}

months = 120

}

		name = "It looks like the oil prices will rise"

set_global_flag = raise_oil_prices

					}
		}

#Biological Weapons spread
country_event = {
	id = 1412064
	title = "Biological Weapons spreads to our nation"
	desc = "A nation has been struck by biological weapons and the agents have been highly infectious allowing it to spread to $COUNTRY$ due to our proximity to a nation which is currently infected with the agents."
	picture = "agent_spreads"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = spreading_bio_weapon }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = biological_attack }
		any_neighbor_country = { has_country_flag = spreading_bio_weapon has_country_modifier = biological_attack }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 2

		modifier = { factor = 4 AND = { immigration_policy = nobody_gets_out war = no } }

		modifier = { factor = 2 AND = { immigration_policy = quota_immigration war = no } }

		modifier = { factor = 2 health_care = good_health_care }
		modifier = { factor = 1.5 health_care = acceptable_health_care }
		modifier = { factor = 1.25 health_care = low_health_care }
	}

	option = {
		name = "We need to find a vaccine for it!"
		prestige = -25
		set_country_flag = spreading_bio_weapon
		add_country_modifier = { name = biological_attack duration = 3650 }
	}
}

		name = "Accept the Conference (Grant Independence)"

		prestige = -50
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "Demand Independence Vote First"
		prestige = -25
		FROM = { country_event = 1412069 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = socialist ruling_party_ideology = progressive ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Reject any attempts to leave!"
		FROM = { country_event = 1412067 }
		prestige = -5
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } }
	}
}

#Puppet Requests Independence
country_event = {
	id = 1412067
	title = "$COUNTRY$ Self-Determination Rejected"
	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ has rejected our request for self determination. This means that we have to declare a War of Independence if we want to secede from our overlord."
	picture = "independence_rejected"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "Fine!"
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 modifier = { factor = 0 has_recently_lost_war = no } }
		prestige = -10
		add_country_modifier = { name = revolution_chaos duration = 365 }
		any_pop = { 
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.2
				value = nationalist
			} 
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "WARR!"
		add_country_modifier = { name = revolution_chaos duration = 365 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 modifier = { factor = 0 has_recently_lost_war = yes } }
		FROM = { release_vassal = THIS }
		any_pop = { 
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.1
				value = nationalist
			} 
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { OR = { has_country_flag = colonial_province has_country_flag = former_colonial_province } } }
			owner = {
				war = {
					target = FROM
					defender_goal = { casus_belli = colonial_war }
					attacker_goal = { casus_belli = become_independent }
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { OR = { has_country_flag = colonial_province has_country_flag = former_colonial_province } } } }
			owner = {
				war = {
					target = FROM
					defender_goal = { }
					attacker_goal = { casus_belli = become_independent }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 1412070
	title = "$YEAR$ $COUNTRY_ADJ$ Independence Referendum"
	desc = "Our independence vote to determine if the people want independence is underway. We will win if conservatives, liberals, progressives or centrists are not the majority ideology in $COUNTRY$. We will know the result in approximately half a month."
	picture = "independence_vote"

	trigger = {
		is_vassal = yes
		has_country_flag = hold_independence_referendum
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6
	}

	option = {
		name = "We hope for the best"
		any_pop = { militancy = -5 }
		clr_country_flag = hold_independence_referendum
		remove_country_modifier = independence_vote_permission
		
		#If there was a stray flag
		clr_country_flag = independence_vote_passes_flag
		
		#Vote Fails
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = {
					NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = populist pop_majority_ideology = socialist pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = communist pop_majority_ideology = communist_social } }
				} 
			}
			owner = { country_event = 1412071 } #Vote fails
			
		}
		
		#Vote passes
		random_owned = {
			limit = { 
				owner = {
					OR = { pop_majority_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = populist pop_majority_ideology = socialist pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = communist pop_majority_ideology = communist_social }
				} 
			}
			owner = { country_event = 1412072 } #Vote fails
			
		}
		
		
	}
	
}

#Start of Factionalism
country_event = {
	id = 1412074
	title = "Death of the $MONARCHTITLE$"
	desc = EVTDESC1412074
	picture = "great_leader_killed"

	trigger = {

		#Any government with President for Life
		has_country_flag = president_for_life
		
		#Monarchies do not have presidents so they are to use Regency & Monarch death systems instead
		NOT = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } }

		#Historical
		NOT = { AND = { tag = SPA government = nationalist_dictatorship NOT = { year = 1985 } } }

		NOT = { AND = { tag = POR government = nationalist_dictatorship NOT = { year = 1975 } } }

		NOT = { AND = { tag = RUS OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 } NOT = { year = 1990 } } }

		NOT = { AND = { tag = CHI government = proletarian_dictatorship NOT = { year = 1975 } } }

		NOT = { AND = { tag = NKO government = proletarian_dictatorship NOT = { year = 1990 } } }

		NOT = { AND = { tag = DAI government = proletarian_dictatorship NOT = { year = 1980 } } }

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = power_vacuum }

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = government_consensus }

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 360
	}

	option = {
		name = "It is a day of mourning"
		
		#Clear President for Life, new dictator has to earn his eternal presidency. If democratic then life term ends, new guy to take over and earn his life term
		clr_country_flag = president_for_life

		#If leader refused to leave via 'backbencher's plot' event
		clr_country_flag = leader_refuses_to_leave

		remove_country_modifier = expert_diplomat
		remove_country_modifier = successful_industrialist
		remove_country_modifier = ivory_tower_intellectual
		remove_country_modifier = man_of_the_people
		remove_country_modifier = landed_gentleman
		remove_country_modifier = military_man
		remove_country_modifier = lord_admiral
		remove_country_modifier = raving_loon
		remove_country_modifier = luddite
		remove_country_modifier = great_statesman
		remove_country_modifier = backroom_boy
		remove_country_modifier = great_reformer
		remove_country_modifier = gauche_buffoon
		remove_country_modifier = administrative_genius
		remove_country_modifier = visionary_thinker
		remove_country_modifier = competent_placeholder
		remove_country_modifier = imperious_autocrat
		remove_country_modifier = prince_of_terror
		remove_country_modifier = efficient_sociopath
		remove_country_modifier = pig_headed_isolationist
		remove_country_modifier = ambitious_union_boss
		remove_country_modifier = dour_economist

		clr_country_flag = right_set_up
		clr_country_flag = far_right_set_up
		clr_country_flag = centre_set_up
		clr_country_flag = left_set_up
		clr_country_flag = far_left_set_up

		add_country_modifier = { name = power_vacuum duration = 730 }

		any_pop = {
			consciousness = 2
			militancy = 1
		}
	}
	
}

#Debate over the Successor - stage 1
country_event = {
	id = 1412075
	title = "$YEAR$ Congress to select new $MONARCHTITLE$"
	desc = EVTDESC1412075
	picture = "great_leader_selection"

	trigger = {

		OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = nationalist_dictatorship government = sectarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 government = theocracy }

		has_country_modifier = power_vacuum

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = factionalism }

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = government_consensus }

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }

	option = {
		name = "Let the leadership contest begin!"
		add_country_modifier = { name = factionalism duration = 1825 }
		country_event = 111222
	}

}

#Choice for the new dictator
country_event = {
	id = 1412076
	title = "Speech by the New $MONARCHTITLE$"
	desc = EVTDESC1412076
	picture = "new_dictator_speech"

	trigger = {

		OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = nationalist_dictatorship government = sectarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 government = theocracy }

		has_country_modifier = factionalism
		has_country_modifier = power_vacuum

		NOT = { has_country_flag = leadership_election }

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }

	option = {
		name = "I will preserve the status quo!"

		remove_country_modifier = power_vacuum

		#Elites will be happy
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { OR = { type = officers type = aristocrats type = bureaucrats } }
			militancy = -10
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.6 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "I will crush the counter-revolutionaries!"
		badboy = 2
		prestige_factor = -0.025
		country_event = 1412077
		remove_country_modifier = power_vacuum
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.4 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "I will start immediate political reforms!"
		prestige_factor = -0.1
		
		#Enact democratic reforms
		political_reform = parties_restricted
		political_reform = semi_democratic_state_opinion
		
		#Remove Power Vacuum
		remove_country_modifier = power_vacuum

		#Coup risk
		add_country_modifier = { name = coup_risk duration = 1825 }

		#Elites get angry
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { OR = { type = officers type = aristocrats type = bureaucrats } }
			militancy = 10 
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

}

#GP Trade Deal
country_event = {
	id = 1412083
	title = "$COUNTRY_ADJ$-$FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Free Trade Deal"
	desc = EVTDESC1412083
	picture = "free_trade_deal"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = "Accept!"
		prestige = 25
		FROM = { prestige = 25 }
		relation = { who = FROM value = 25 }
		FROM = { add_country_modifier = { name = bilateral_trade_pact_gp duration = 1825 } }
		add_country_modifier = { name = bilateral_trade_pact_gp duration = 1825 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "Reject!"
		FROM = { country_event = 1412085 }
		prestige = -10
		add_country_modifier = { name = trade_deal_failure duration = 500 }
		relation = { who = FROM value = -25 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}
}

						NOT = { badboy = 1 }
					}
					country_event = 1412088
				}
			}
			50 = { 
				#Normal

					limit = {
						has_country_modifier = united_nations_ga_member
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = unsc_permanent_member }

					}

				}
			}
			25 = { 
				#Passive

					limit = {
						has_country_modifier = united_nations_ga_member
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = unsc_permanent_member }

					}

			}
		}
	}

#Financial Crisis
country_event = {
	id = 1412094
	title = "Financial Meltdown in $COUNTRY$"
	desc = EVTDESC1412094
	picture = "financial_crisis"

	trigger = {
	
		#Favourable economic condition
		OR = {
			money = 5000000
			has_country_modifier = economic_boom
		}

		#Post 2000s
		modern_stock_exchange = 1
		
		#Appropriate economic policy
		OR = {
			economic_policy = laissez_faire
			economic_policy = interventionism
			AND = { economic_policy = state_capitalism has_country_modifier = stock_market_crash }
		}
		
		#Does not have high baking regulations
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = bkrhigh }
		
		#Does not already have an economic crisis in THIS
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = financial_crisis }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = recession }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = great_recession }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = great_depression }
		
		#Only 1 financial crisis at a time
		NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { has_country_modifier = great_recession } }
		NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { has_country_modifier = recession } }
		NOT = { any_greater_power = { has_country_modifier = great_recession } }

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3650
		modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_modifier = bkrlow }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 has_country_modifier = bkrmedium }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Bail the banks out, we can't afford a meltdown"
		add_tax_relative_income = -50

		#Prestige loss
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = yes } }
			owner = { prestige_factor = -0.02 }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = no } }
			owner = { prestige_factor = -0.02 }
		}
		
		#Pops want less government intervention in the economy
		any_pop = {
			dominant_issue = {
				value = laissez_faire
				factor = 0.15
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.8
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				economic_policy = laissez_faire
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Let the market restructure itself"
		
		capitalists = { money = -1000 }
		aristocrats = { money = -500 }
		
		#Prestige loss
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = yes } }
			owner = { prestige_factor = -0.02 }
		}
		
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = no } }
			owner = { prestige_factor = -0.02 }
		}
		
		#Pops want more government intervention in the economy
		any_pop = {
			dominant_issue = {
				value = interventionism
				factor = 0.15
			}
		}
		
		#Economic contagion to the whole world if a rank 2 and above GP
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = yes rank = 2 } }
			owner = { 
			
				add_country_modifier = { name = great_recession duration = 1000 }
			
				any_country = {
					limit = { 
					
						exists = yes
					
						#Appropriate economic policy
						OR = {
							economic_policy = laissez_faire
							economic_policy = interventionism
							AND = { economic_policy = state_capitalism has_country_modifier = stock_market_crash }
						}
		
						#Does not have high baking regulations
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = bkrhigh }
		
						#Does not already have an economic crisis in THIS
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = financial_crisis }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = recession }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = great_recession }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = great_depression }
					}
					#Economic Contagion - Great Recession
					country_event = 1412095
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Economic contagion to the whole world if a rank 4 and below GP
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = yes NOT = { rank = 2 } } }
			owner = { 
			
				add_country_modifier = { name = recession duration = 900 }
			
				any_country = {
					limit = { 
					
						exists = yes
					
						#Appropriate economic policy
						OR = {
							economic_policy = laissez_faire
							economic_policy = interventionism
							AND = { economic_policy = state_capitalism has_country_modifier = stock_market_crash }
						}
		
						#Does not have high baking regulations
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = bkrhigh }
		
						#Does not already have an economic crisis in THIS
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = financial_crisis }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = recession }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = great_recession }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = great_depression }
					}
					#Economic Contagion - Normal Recession
					country_event = 1412096
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Economic contagion to the whole region if is an SP
		#europe
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { is_secondary_power = yes capital_scope = { continent = europe } } }
			owner = { 
			
				add_country_modifier = { name = recession duration = 900 }
			
				any_country = {
					limit = { 
					
						exists = yes
						
						capital_scope = { continent = europe }
					
						#Appropriate economic policy
						OR = {
							economic_policy = laissez_faire
							economic_policy = interventionism
							AND = { economic_policy = state_capitalism has_country_modifier = stock_market_crash }
						}
		
						#Does not have high baking regulations
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = bkrhigh }
		
						#Does not already have an economic crisis in THIS
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = financial_crisis }

					country_event = 1412096
				}
			}
		}

						}

						NOT = { has_country_modifier = financial_crisis }

# Great Recession for all eligible
country_event = {
	id = 1412095
	title = "The Great Recession of $YEAR$"
	desc = EVT_1412095_DESC
	picture = "financial_crisis"
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVT_1412095_A # "We will have to tide through this"
		prestige_factor = -0.02
		add_tax_relative_income = -50

		capitalists = { money = -1000 }
		aristocrats = { money = -500 }

		add_country_modifier = { name = great_recession duration = 1000 }
	}
}


# Financial crisis for all in region
country_event = {
	id = 1412096
	title = "The Financial Crisis of $YEAR$"
	desc = EVT_1412095_DESC
	picture = "financial_crisis"
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVT_1412095_A
		prestige_factor = -0.01
		add_tax_relative_income = -25
		
		capitalists = { money = -500 }
		aristocrats = { money = -250 }
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = recession duration = 900 }
	}
}

# German Reparations
country_event = {
	id = 1412097
	title = "German War Reparations"
	desc = EVTDESC1412097
	picture = "german_reparations"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = { tag = GER tag = FRG }
		NOT = { year = 1991 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "As the losers, we have no choice"
		prestige = -10
		add_country_modifier = { name = ger_war_rep duration = 23360 }
	}
}

#Rise of the Metropolitan elite
country_event = {
	id = 1412100
	title = "Rise of the Metropolitan Elite"
	desc = "Due to the increasingly powerful role that the cities in $COUNTRY$ play to the national economy, they have started to gain an increasingly disproportionate amount of political representation and influence in $COUNTRY$."
	picture = "city_voting_more"

	trigger = {
		globalization = 1
		NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = city_politics_boost } }
		OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 7300 
		modifier = { factor = 0.4 vote_franschise = free_voting }
		modifier = { factor = 0.8 vote_franschise = gerrymandered_voting }
		modifier = { factor = 1.5 vote_franschise = rigged_voting } 
		modifier = { factor = 3 vote_franschise = harassed_voting } 
	}

	option = {
		name = "The City rules"
		any_owned = { limit = { 
				OR = { is_capital = yes AND = { is_state_capital = yes total_pops = 1000000 } } 
			} 
			add_province_modifier = { name = city_politics_boost duration = -1 } }
	}
}

#End of the Metropolitan elite
country_event = {
	id = 1412101
	title = "End of the Metropolitan Elite"
	desc = "As we are no longer a proper demcracy, the cities' disproportionate amount of political representation and influence in $COUNTRY$ have been lost to the central government."
	picture = "city_voting_less"

	trigger = {
		globalization = 1
		any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = city_politics_boost }
		NOT = { OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "The City loses"
		any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = city_politics_boost }
	}
}

#Special Drawing Rights
country_event = {
	id = 1412102
	title = "Special Drawing Rights Revoked"
	desc = "As we are either no longer a substantial global power or a proper functioning capitalist system, the IMF has decided to withdraw our SDR to prevent misuse of it."
	picture = "sdr_revoked"

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = special_imf_dr
		OR = { government = theocracy government = proletarian_dictatorship government = proletarian_dictatorship1 is_greater_power = no NOT = { has_country_modifier = imf_member } NOT = { any_owned_province = { trade_goods = credit } } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "A loss for our nation"
		clr_country_flag = special_imf_dr
		prestige = -25
		any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = imf_sdr }
	}
}

#South Vietnam Reunification
country_event = {
	id = 1412103
	title = "Reunification of Vietnam"
	desc = EVTDESC1412103
	picture = "vietnam_svi_reunion"

	trigger = {
		tag = SVI
		NOT = { exists = DAI }
		owns = 1369
		owns = 1380
	}

	option = {
		name = "Let's celebrate!"
		
		#Clear cores
		SVI = { all_core = { add_core = DAI remove_core = SVI } }
		
		change_tag = DAI
		prestige = 50
	}
}

#Dissolution of the TTPI
country_event = {
	id = 1412104
	title = "Dissolution of $COUNTRY$?"
	desc = EVTDESC1412104 # TODO Change this to mention that, in becoming Micronesia, three out of seven countries elected not to join
	picture = "ttip_end"
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = XPI
		USA = { exists = yes government = democracy }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				year = 2010
				OR = {
					ruling_party_ideology = nationalist
					any_owned_province = { controlled_by_rebels = yes }
					militancy = 8
				}
			}
			is_vassal = no
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 4 }

	option = {
		name = "Dissolve the federation!"

		release = PAU

		release = MAR

		NMI = { random_country = { limit = { tag = THIS NOT = { exists = NMI } } release = NMI USA = { diplomatic_influence = { who = NMI value = 200 } } } }

		change_tag = MIC

		USA = { create_vassal = PAU }

		USA = { create_vassal = MAR }

		USA = { create_vassal = NMI }

		PAU = { government = mandate_government country_event = 800054 }

		MAR = { government = mandate_government country_event = 800054 }

		NMI = { government = sar_government country_event = 800054 ruling_party_ideology = conservative }

		USA = { diplomatic_influence = { who = PAU value = 200 } }
	
		USA = { diplomatic_influence = { who = MAR value = 200 } }
	
		USA = { diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = 200 } }

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.8
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_secondary_power = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				rank = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				year = 2010
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Keep the federation!"
		primary_culture = micronesian
		prestige = 30
		NMI = {
			any_owned = { add_core = THIS } # If coming from USA
			overlord = { relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
		}
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = MIC } 
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = nationalist_agitation duration = 1095 }
			any_pop = {
				militancy = 10
				consciousness = 8
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.2 }
	}
	
}

#Dissolution of the TTPI
country_event = {
	id = 1412105
	title = "Independence of the Pacific Islands?"
	desc = EVTDESC1412104
	picture = "ttip_end"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		year = 1985
		XPI = { government = mandate_government }
		is_our_vassal = XPI
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 1986
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Grant independence!"
		release_vassal = XPI
		prestige = 10
		XPI = {
			government = democracy
			release = NMI
			country_event = 1412104
		}
		NMI = { government = democracy }
		create_vassal = NMI
		diplomatic_influence = { who = NMI value = 200 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ruling_party_ideology = populist
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Refuse independence!"
		prestige_factor = -0.1
		badboy = 2.5
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.05
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				badboy = 0.9
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					ruling_party_ideology = progressive
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
